[Personality]

[Conversation Style]

from fastapi import FastAPI
from fastapi.middleware.cors import CORSMiddleware
from director_core.models import AnalyzeRequest
from director_core.main import analyze_text_with_llm

app = FastAPI()

app.add_middleware(
    CORSMiddleware,
    allow_origins=["*"],
    allow_credentials=True,
    allow_methods=["*"],
    allow_headers=["*"],
)
